	// Conjurer's Conjure Image

		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_NO"
		"AbilityCastAnimation"			"ACT_DOTA_CAST_ABILITY_4"
		"AbilityCastPoint"				"0.25"
		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"

		"AbilityManaCost"				"100 110 120 130"

	// Gives team gold when killed (because its a npc_dota_creature which doesn't trigger the tower gold by default)
	// Also checks the tree of life to see if glyph was used (because the built in even doesn't work)
	"dota_radiant_tower"
	{
		"BaseClass" 		"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior" 	"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_PASSIVE | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_HIDDEN"
	
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_tower_gold"
			{
				"Passive"   "1"
				"IsHidden"	"1"
				"OnDeath"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"buildings/tower.lua"
						"Function"		"GiveTeamTowerGold"
					}
				}
			}
	
			"modifier_tower_glyph"	
			{
				"Passive"   "1"
				"IsHidden"	"1"
	
				"OnCreated"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"buildings/tower.lua"
						"Function"		"FindTreeOfLife"
					}
				}
	
				"ThinkInterval"  "0.03"
				"OnIntervalThink"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"buildings/tower.lua"
						"Function"		"CheckGlyphUsage"
					}
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	// Tower Properties:
	//	Truesight
	//	Invulnerability before 0:00
	//	Protects the ancient (2 instances in this case)
	//	Backdoor protection (not really that important in such a small map)
	"dota_tower_creature"
	{
		"BaseClass" 		"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior" 	"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_PASSIVE | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_HIDDEN"
	
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_tower"
			{
				"Passive"   "1"
				"IsHidden"	"1"
				"States"
				{
					"MODIFIER_STATE_MAGIC_IMMUNE"       	"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
				}
	
				"OnCreated"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"buildings/tower.lua"
						"Function"		"ApplyInvulnerability"
					}
	
					"ApplyModifier"
					{
						"ModifierName"	"modifier_tower_truesight_aura"
						"Target" 		"CASTER"
					}
				}
	
				"OnDestroy"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"buildings/tower.lua"
						"Function"		"ReduceInvulnerabilityCount"
					}
				}
	
				"ThinkInterval"  "0.03"
				"OnIntervalThink"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"buildings/tower.lua"
						"Function"		"InvulnerabilityCheck"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	// Gambler's All in
	// Author: Noya
	// Date: March 25, 2015
	// Deals anywhere from 1 to his gold in damage. If it fails, loses a random amount of his gold
	"gambler_retro_all_in"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_UNIT_TARGET"
		"AbilityUnitTargetTeam"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_ENEMY"
		"AbilityUnitTargetType"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO"
		"AbilityTextureName" 			"gambler_retro_all_in"
		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_NO"
		"AbilityCastAnimation"			"ACT_DOTA_CAST_ABILITY_4"
		"AbilityType"					"DOTA_ABILITY_TYPE_ULTIMATE"
		"AbilityUnitDamageType"			"DAMAGE_TYPE_PURE"
		"AbilityCastPoint"				"0.25"
		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCooldown"				"60"
		"AbilityManaCost"				"150"
		"AbilityCastRange"				"600"
	
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"		"particles/units/heroes/hero_gambler/gambler_all_in_success.vpcf"
			"particle"		"particles/units/heroes/hero_gambler/gambler_all_in_failure.vpcf"
			"particle"		"particles/units/heroes/hero_gambler/gambler_all_in_failure_coins.vpcf"
			"particle"		"particles/units/heroes/hero_gambler/gambler_all_in_success_coins.vpcf"
			"particle"		"particles/units/heroes/hero_gambler/gambler_all_in_failure_gold_lost_msg.vpcf"
			"particle"		"particles/units/heroes/hero_gambler/gambler_all_in_success_damage_msg.vpcf"
			"particle"		"particles/units/heroes/hero_gambler/gambler_all_in_success_explosion.vpcf"
			"soundfile"		"soundevents/custom_sounds.vsndevts"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"damage_cap"			"1500 2000 2500"  
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"chance_to_fail"		"30 25 20"	
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"pip_show"				"0"
			}
		}
	
		"OnSpellStart"
		{	
			"Random"
			{
				"Chance"			"100 - %chance_to_fail"
				"OnSuccess"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_gambler/all_in.lua"
						"Function"		"AllInSuccess"
					}
				}
				"OnFailure"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_gambler/all_in.lua"
						"Function"		"AllInFailure"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	// Gambler's Ante up
	// Author: wFX
	// Date: March 16, 2015
	// Gambler wagers 100 gold on the game targeting a hero.
	// If the target get a kill first, Gambler cashes in for a big reward,
	// If the target dies first, Gambler cashes in for half as much.
	// Damages enemy, heal allies.
	// Cash in for 300 400 500 600, damage/heal for 50 100 150 200
	// Lua code have a workaround for prevent self casting
	
	"gambler_retro_ante_up"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_UNIT_TARGET"
		"AbilityUnitTargetTeam"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_ENEMY | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_FRIENDLY"
		"AbilityUnitTargetType"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO"
		"AbilityTextureName" 			"gambler_retro_ante_up"
		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_NO"
		"MaxLevel"						"4"
		"AbilityUnitDamageType"			"DAMAGE_TYPE_MAGICAL"

	// Gambler's Lucky Stars
	// Author: wFX
	// Date: March 16, 2015
	// 5 6 7 8% of chance on auto attack to 
	// Instantly kill a creep
	// Deal 200 extra damage on buildings and on heroes
	// Also always pillage gold with the formula
	// (AttackDamage/TargetMaxHP) * PillageRatio * TargetBounty/2
	
	"gambler_retro_lucky_stars"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_PASSIVE"

		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_YES"
		"AbilityTextureName"			"gambler_retro_lucky_stars"
		
		// Precache
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"precache"
		 {
			"particle"		"particles/units/heroes/hero_gambler/gambler_lucky_stars_lucky.vpcf"
			"particle"		"particles/units/heroes/hero_life_stealer/life_stealer_open_wounds_blood_firstpool.vpcf"
		 }
	
		// Special

	// Invoker's Betrayal
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: February 15, 2015
	// Invoke: Quas Wex Quas
	// Cast a dark magic on a target enemy, causing all of its previous allies to turn against it, thinking it's a foe. Duration based on Quas.
	// To do: Prevent the Betrayed unit from damaging their former allies, possibly using an OnTakeDamage event.  It may be impossible to give the Betrayed unit their original team's vision.
	"invoker_retro_betrayal"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_UNIT_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NOT_LEARNABLE"
		"AbilityUnitTargetTeam"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_ENEMY"
		"AbilityUnitTargetType"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO"
		"AbilityTextureName" 			"invoker_retro_betrayal"
		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_NO"
		"AbilityCastAnimation" 			"ACT_DOTA_CAST_COLD_SNAP"
		"FightRecapLevel"				"1"
		"MaxLevel"						"1"
		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCooldown"				"20"
		"AbilityManaCost"				"200"
		"AbilityCastRange"				"500"
		
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"				"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_betrayal.vpcf"
			"particle"				"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_betrayal_explosion.vpcf"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"duration"				"1.5 3 4.5 6 7.5 9 10.5 12"  //Increases with Quas.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"			"1"
			}
		}

			{
				"ScriptFile"		"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_betrayal.lua"

			}
		}

		{
			"modifier_invoker_retro_betrayal"

				"Duration"			"%duration"
				"Passive"  			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"0"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"1"
				"IsPurgable"		"1"
				
				"EffectName"			"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_betrayal.vpcf"
				"EffectAttachType"		"follow_overhead"
				
				//When this modifier's duration ends, or when it is othwerwise removed, move the affected unit back to their original team.
				"OnDestroy"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"		"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_betrayal.lua"
						"Function"			"modifier_invoker_retro_betrayal_on_destroy"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	// Invoker's Chaos Meteor
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: February 27, 2015
	// Invoke: Exort Quas Quas
	// Summons a powerful meteor to crush all enemies within its path. Deals 200 damage per second to units in its path. Based on Exort.
	// Note: Different sources indicate different damage values.  Some say it deals 25 damage per level of Exort per second to units in its path,
	//     while others say the meteor itself deals 50/100/150/200/250/300/350/400 DPS and its path burns for 5 seconds, dealing a flat 80 damage per second.
	"invoker_retro_chaos_meteor"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_POINT | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NOT_LEARNABLE"
		"AbilityTextureName" 			"invoker_retro_chaos_meteor"
		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_NO"
		"AbilityUnitDamageType"			"DAMAGE_TYPE_MAGICAL"
		"AbilityCastAnimation" 			"ACT_DOTA_CAST_CHAOS_METEOR"
		"FightRecapLevel"				"1"
		"MaxLevel"						"1"
		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCooldown"				"20"
		"AbilityManaCost"				"200"
		"AbilityCastRange"				"700"
		
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"				"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_chaos_meteor.vpcf"
			"particle"				"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_chaos_meteor_fly.vpcf"
			"particle"				"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_chaos_meteor_burn_debuff.vpcf"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"land_delay"						"1.3"  //The meteor lands on the ground this many seconds after it was cast.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"travel_distance"					"1500"  //Given a 300 travel speed and a 1500 travel distance, the meteor rolls for 5 seconds.
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"travel_speed"						"300"  //Given a 300 travel speed and a 1500 travel distance, the meteor rolls for 5 seconds.
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"vision_distance"					"500"  //This is flying vision given by the meteor ball.
			}
			"05"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"end_vision_duration"				"3.0"  //The meteor's flying vision lingers for this long after it disappears.
			}
			"06"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"main_damage_radius"				"275"  //This is the radius of the meteor ball.
			}
			"07"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"main_damage_interval"				"0.5"  //The main meteor ball deals its damage and applies its DoT burn every main_damage_interval.  Modify main_damage_per_second_tooltip is this is.
			}
			"08"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"main_damage_per_interval"			"25 50 75 100 125 150 175 200"  //Increases with Exort.  This is the damage dealt by the meteor ball every main_damage_interval.  Several instances of this damage value can be applied to enemies who follow the meteor's path.  Modify main_damage_per_second_tooltip is this is.
			}
			"09"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"main_damage_per_second_tooltip"	"50 100 150 200 250 300 350 400"
			}
			"10"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"burn_duration"						"5"  //Units hit by the meteor receive a modifier lasting this many seconds that regularly damages them.
			}
			"11"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"burn_damage_per_interval"			"80"  //Units who are hit by the meteor also have a modifier applied to them that deals this much damage per interval.  I don't think there's a mechanic where the meteor leaves a trail behind it that damages units standing in it.
			}
			"12"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"burn_interval"						"1.0"  //Alter the tooltip if this is changed.
			}
			"13"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"			"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"								"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_chaos_meteor.lua"
				"Function"									"invoker_retro_chaos_meteor_on_spell_start"
				"Target"									"POINT"
				"LandDelay"									"%land_delay"
				"TravelDistance"							"%travel_distance"
				"TravelSpeed"								"%travel_speed"
				"VisionDistance"							"%vision_distance"
				"EndVisionDuration"							"%end_vision_duration"
			}
		}
		
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_invoker_retro_chaos_meteor_main_damage"
			{
				"Passive"  			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"1"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				
				"ThinkInterval" 	"%main_damage_interval"
				"OnIntervalThink"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_chaos_meteor.lua"
						"Function"				"modifier_invoker_retro_chaos_meteor_main_damage_on_interval_think"
						"MainDamageRadius"		"%main_damage_radius"
					}
				}
				
				"OnCreated"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_chaos_meteor.lua"
						"Function"				"modifier_invoker_retro_chaos_meteor_main_damage_on_interval_think"
						"MainDamageRadius"		"%main_damage_radius"
					}
				}
			}
			"modifier_invoker_retro_chaos_meteor_burn_damage"
			{
				"Duration"			"%burn_duration"
				"Passive"  			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"0"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"1"
				"IsPurgable"		"1"
				
				"ThinkInterval" 	"%burn_interval"
				"OnIntervalThink"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_chaos_meteor.lua"
						"Function"				"modifier_invoker_retro_chaos_meteor_burn_damage_on_interval_think"
						"BurnDamagePerInterval"	"%burn_damage_per_interval"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"travel_distance"					"1500"  //Given a 300 travel speed and a 1500 travel distance, the meteor rolls for 5 seconds.
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"travel_speed"						"300"  //Given a 300 travel speed and a 1500 travel distance, the meteor rolls for 5 seconds.
			}

			}
			"07"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"

			}
			"08"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"

			}

			}
			"12"

	// Invoker's Confuse

	// Invoker's Deafening Blast
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: March 5, 2015
	// Invoke: Exort Exort Quas
	// Hits an enemy unit with a defeaning blast, dealing heavy damage and causing the target to be mute for 3.5 seconds. Deals 65 damage per level in Exort.
	"invoker_retro_deafening_blast"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_UNIT_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NOT_LEARNABLE"
		"AbilityUnitTargetTeam"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_ENEMY"
		"AbilityUnitTargetType"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_CREEP"
		"AbilityTextureName" 			"invoker_retro_deafening_blast"
		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_NO"
		"AbilityCastAnimation" 			"ACT_DOTA_CAST_COLD_SNAP"
		"FightRecapLevel"				"1"
		"MaxLevel"						"1"
		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCooldown"				"20"
		"AbilityManaCost"				"350"
		"AbilityCastRange"				"700"
		
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"			"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_deafening_blast_debuff.vpcf"
			"particle"			"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_deafening_blast_impact.vpcf"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"mute_duration"			"1.5 2 2.5 3 3.5 4 4.5 5"  //Increases with Exort.
			}
	
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"damage"				"65 130 195 260 325 390 455 520"  //Increases with Exort.
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"			"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_deafening_blast.lua"
				"Function"				"invoker_retro_deafening_blast_on_spell_start"
			}
			
			"FireEffect"
			{
				"EffectName"           "particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_deafening_blast_impact.vpcf"
				"EffectAttachType"     "PATTACH_ABSORIGIN_FOLLOW"
				"Target"               "TARGET"
			}
		}
	
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_invoker_retro_deafening_blast"
			{
				"Passive"			"0"
				"IsHidden"			"0"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"1"
				"IsPurgable"		"1"
				"TextureName"		"invoker_retro_deafening_blast"
				
				"EffectName"            "particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_deafening_blast_debuff.vpcf"
				"EffectAttachType"      "PATTACH_ABSORIGIN"
	
				"States"
				{
					"MODIFIER_STATE_MUTED"  				"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
					"MODIFIER_STATE_SILENCED"				"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
					"MODIFIER_STATE_PASSIVES_DISABLED"		"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
				}
				
				"OnCreated"
				{
					"AttachEffect"
					{
						"Target"			"TARGET"
						"EffectName"		"particles/generic_gameplay/generic_silence.vpcf"
						"EffectAttachType"	"follow_overhead"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	// Invoker's Disarm
	// Author: wFX
	// Date: February 15, 2015
	// Invoke: Exort Quas Exort
	// Strips the enemy of the capability to attack. Lasts up to 8 seconds with 1200 cast range. Duration and cast range based on Exort.
	// Balance Ideas: Make cast range based on Quas

	// Invoker's EMP
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: February 24, 2015
	// Invoke: Wex Quas Wex
	// Releases an EMP bomb that detonates depleting the mana of all enemies nearby. Up to 640 mana per unit based on Wex and Quas levels.
	"invoker_retro_emp"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NO_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NOT_LEARNABLE"
		"AbilityTextureName" 			"invoker_retro_emp"
		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_NO"
		"AbilityCastAnimation" 			"ACT_DOTA_CAST_EMP"
		"FightRecapLevel"				"1"
		"MaxLevel"						"1"
		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCooldown"				"30"
		"AbilityManaCost"				"200"
		
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"			"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_emp.vpcf"
			"particle"			"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_emp_explode.vpcf"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"						"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"distance_to_move"				"600"  //Note that the particle spawns 100 units in front of Invoker.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"						"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"projectile_speed_per_second"	"200"
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"						"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"delay_before_exploding"		"2.0"  //This delay begins once the EMP has reached its final position.
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"						"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"radius"						"600"
			}
			"05"
			{
				"var_type"						"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"mana_burned"					"100 200 300 400 500 600 700 800"  //Increases with Quas and Wex.
			}
			"06"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"			"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"					"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_emp.lua"
				"Function"						"invoker_retro_emp_on_spell_start"
				"DistanceToMove"				"%distance_to_move"
				"ProjectileSpeedPerSecond"		"%projectile_speed_per_second"
				"DelayBeforeExploding"			"%delay_before_exploding"
				"Radius"						"%radius"
			}
		}
	}

	{
		// General

	// Invoker's Energy Ball
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: March 5, 2015
	// Invoke: Wex Exort Wex
	// Summons an energy ball that explodes dealing up to 800 damage to units in a 400 AOE based on Wex level.
	"invoker_retro_energy_ball"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NO_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NOT_LEARNABLE"

		"AbilityManaCost"				"250"

			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"								"FIELD_FLOAT"

			}

			"04"

	// Invoker's Exort
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: February 15, 2015
	// Builds Kael's skill in the fire magics. These spells, when invoked, deal with the power of fire, projection and damage. As a reagent, regenerates .5 hitpoints per level, per reagent cast. Increases Strength by 1 each time his skill is learned.
	"invoker_retro_exort"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NO_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_IMMEDIATE | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_IGNORE_BACKSWING"

		"MaxLevel"						"8"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

		"AbilityManaCost"				"0"

		{
			"particle"			"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_exort_orb.vpcf"
			"soundfile"			"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_invoker.vsndevts"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"bonus_health_regen_per_instance"	".5 1.0 1.5 2.0 2.5 3.0 3.5 4"
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"bonus_strength"					"1 2 3 4 5 6 7 8"
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"								"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_show"								"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{

			}

			}
		}

			}
		}

	// Invoker's Firestorm
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: March 6, 2015
	// Invoke: Exort Wex Wex
	// Calls then magical fireballs from the sky to land around Kael. Deals 30 damage to units that lay beneath it and leaves a magical Fireball remaining. This unit damages nearby units with fire, with damage and AOE based on your Exort level. When Fireball expires, it deals 150 AOE damage.
	"invoker_retro_firestorm"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_AOE | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_POINT | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NOT_LEARNABLE"
		"AbilityTextureName" 			"invoker_retro_firestorm"
		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_NO"
		"AbilityUnitDamageType"			"DAMAGE_TYPE_MAGICAL"
		"AbilityCastAnimation" 			"ACT_DOTA_CAST_ICE_WALL"
		"FightRecapLevel"				"1"
		"MaxLevel"						"1"
		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCooldown"				"30"
		"AbilityManaCost"				"250"
		"AbilityCastRange"				"550"
		"AoERadius"						"300"  //Update fireball_cast_radius if this is.
		
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"					"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_firestorm_fireball_fly.vpcf"
			"particle"					"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_firestorm_fireball.vpcf"
			"particle"					"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_firestorm_fireball_explosion.vpcf"
			"particle"					"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_firestorm_fireball_crumble.vpcf"
			"soundfile"					"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_phoenix.vsndevts"
			"soundfile"					"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_earth_spirit.vsndevts"
			"soundfile"					"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_warlock.vsndevts"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"num_fireballs"						"2 4 6 8 10 12 14 16"  //Increases with Exort.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"fireball_land_delay"				".5"  //The time between when the fireball spawns and when it lands.  If this is changed, modify invoker_retro_firestorm_fireball_fly.vpcf's "travel time" under Constraint -> "Constrain distance to path between two control points"
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"fireball_delay_between_spawns"		".25"
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"fireball_cast_radius"				"300"  //Update "AoERadius" if this is.
			}
			"05"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"fireball_damage_aoe"				"200"  //If this is changed, modify several particle effect radii.
			}
			"06"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"fireball_landing_damage"			"30"
			}
			"07"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"fireball_aoe_damage_per_second"	"150"
			}
			"08"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"fireball_aoe_damage_interval"		".5"
			}
			"09"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"fireball_duration"					"7"
			}
			"10"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"fireball_explosion_damage"			"150"
			}
			"11"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"fireball_vision_radius"			"75"
			}
			"12"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"			"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"					"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_firestorm.lua"
				"Function"						"invoker_retro_firestorm_on_spell_start"
				"Target"						"POINT"
				"FireballCastRadius"			"%fireball_cast_radius"
				"FireballLandDelay"				"%fireball_land_delay"
				"FireballDelayBetweenSpawns"	"%fireball_delay_between_spawns"
				"FireballVisionRadius"			"%fireball_vision_radius"
				"FireballDamageAoE"				"%fireball_damage_aoe"
				"FireballLandingDamage"			"%fireball_landing_damage"
				"FireballDuration"				"%fireball_duration"
				"FireballExplosionDamage"		"%fireball_explosion_damage"
			}
		}
		
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_invoker_retro_firestorm_fireball_duration"
			{
				"Passive"  			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"1"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				
				"ThinkInterval" 	".03"
				"OnIntervalThink"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"					"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_firestorm.lua"
						"Function"						"modifier_invoker_retro_firestorm_fireball_duration_on_interval_think"
						"FireballDuration"				"%fireball_duration"
					}
				}
			}		
			//This aura emitter is placed on landed fireballs to make it so the DoTs from multiple fireballs do not stack.
			"modifier_invoker_retro_firestorm_fireball_damage_over_time_aura_emitter"
			{
				"Passive"			"0"
				"IsHidden"			"1"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				"Aura" 				"modifier_invoker_retro_firestorm_fireball_damage_over_time_aura"
				"Aura_Radius" 		"%fireball_damage_aoe"
				"Aura_Teams" 		"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_ENEMY"
				"Aura_Types" 		"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_BASIC"
				"Aura_ApplyToCaster" "0"
			}
			"modifier_invoker_retro_firestorm_fireball_damage_over_time_aura"
			{
				"Passive"			"0"
				"IsHidden"			"0"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"1"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				"TextureName"		"invoker_retro_firestorm"
				
				"ThinkInterval" 	"%fireball_aoe_damage_interval"
				"OnIntervalThink"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"					"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_firestorm.lua"
						"Function"						"modifier_invoker_retro_firestorm_fireball_damage_over_time_aura_on_interval_think"
						"FireballAoEDamageInterval"		"%fireball_aoe_damage_interval"
						"FireballAoEDamagePerSecond"	"%fireball_aoe_damage_per_second"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	// Invoker's Incinerate
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: March 8, 2015
	// Invoke: Exort Wex Exort
	// Does heavy damage to enemy units caught in the area. Range and number of flames increase per level exort. Channeling.
	// This ability is split up into 8 versions since cast range, AoE radius, and channel time scale with Exort.
	
	
	
	//Dummy for popup
	"invoker_retro_incinerate"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_CHANNELLED | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_AOE | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_POINT | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NOT_LEARNABLE"
		"AbilityTextureName" 			"invoker_retro_incinerate"
		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_NO"
		"AbilityUnitDamageType"			"DAMAGE_TYPE_MAGICAL"
		"AbilityCastAnimation" 			"ACT_DOTA_CAST_ICE_WALL"
		"FightRecapLevel"				"1"
		"MaxLevel"						"1"
		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCooldown"				"25"
		"AbilityManaCost"				"200"
		"AbilityCastRange"				"50"  //Update cast_range if this is.
		"AoERadius"						"%wave_radius"
		"AbilityChannelTime"			"1.65"  //Update num_waves and delay_between_waves if this is.  An extra .05 channel time is added as a hack to get the last wave to deal damage.
		
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"					"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.vpcf"
			"soundfile"					"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_warlock.vsndevts"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"cast_range"						"40 80 120 160 200 240 280 320"  //Increases with Exort.  These values are currently hardcoded into AbilityCastRange because it cannot take in AbilitySpecial variables.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"num_waves"							"2 4 6 8 10 12 14 16"  //Increases with Exort.  Update AbilityChannelTime or delay_between_waves if this is.
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"wave_radius"						"50 100 150 200 250 300 350 400"  //Increases with Exort.
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"wave_radius_increase_per_wave"		"0"
			}
			"05"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"damage_per_wave"					"50"
			}
			"06"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"delay_between_waves"				".8"  //The first wave occurs this long after the channeling starts, and subsequent waves have this long of a delay between them, too.  Update AbilityChannelTime or num_waves if this is.
			}
			"07"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"channel_time"						"1.65 3.25 4.85 6.45 8.05 9.65 11.25 12.85"  //These values are currently hardcoded into AbilityChannelTime because it cannot take in AbilitySpecial variables.
			}
			"08"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"						"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.lua"
				"Function"				"invoker_retro_incinerate_on_spell_start"
				"Target"				"POINT"
			}
			
			"ApplyModifier"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation"
	            "Target"				"CASTER"
	        }
		}
		
		"OnChannelFinish"
	    {
	        "RemoveModifier"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation"
	            "Target"				"CASTER"
	        }
			
			"RemoveModifier"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation_override"
	            "Target"				"CASTER"
	        }
			
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.lua"
				"Function"				"invoker_retro_incinerate_on_channel_finish"
			}
	    }
		
		
		"Modifiers"
	    {
			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling"  //Applied to the dummy unit when Invoker begins channeling, and is removed when he stops.
	        {
				"Passive"			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"1"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				
	            "OnCreated"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.lua"
						"Function"				"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_on_created"
						"DelayBetweenWaves"		"%delay_between_waves"
						"DamagePerWave"			"%damage_per_wave"
					}
				}
	        }
			
	        "modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation"  //Repeatedly applies an animation to the caster to make them appear to be channeling.
	        {
				"Passive"			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"1"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				
	            "ThinkInterval"		".6"
	            "OnIntervalThink"
				{
	                "ApplyModifier"
	                {
	                    "ModifierName"		"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation_override"
	                    "Target"			"CASTER"
	                }
	            }
	        }
	
	        "modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation_override"
	        {
				"Duration"			"0.5"
	            "Passive"  			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"1"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				
	            "OverrideAnimation" "ACT_DOTA_CAST_ICE_WALL"
	        }
		}
	}

		"AbilityChannelTime"			"3.25"  //Update num_waves and delay_between_waves if this is.  An extra .05 channel time is added as a hack to get the last wave to deal damage.

		{
			"particle"					"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.vpcf"
			"soundfile"					"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_warlock.vsndevts"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"cast_range"						"40 80 120 160 200 240 280 320"  //Increases with Exort.  These values are currently hardcoded into AbilityCastRange because it cannot take in AbilitySpecial variables.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"num_waves"							"2 4 6 8 10 12 14 16"  //Increases with Exort.  Update AbilityChannelTime or delay_between_waves if this is.
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"wave_radius"						"50 100 150 200 250 300 350 400"  //Increases with Exort.
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"wave_radius_increase_per_wave"		"0"
			}
			"05"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"damage_per_wave"					"50"
			}
			"06"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"delay_between_waves"				".8"  //The first wave occurs this long after the channeling starts, and subsequent waves have this long of a delay between them, too.  Update AbilityChannelTime or num_waves if this is.
			}
			"07"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"channel_time"						"1.65 3.25 4.85 6.45 8.05 9.65 11.25 12.85"  //These values are currently hardcoded into AbilityChannelTime because it cannot take in AbilitySpecial variables.
			}
			"08"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"						"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.lua"
				"Function"				"invoker_retro_incinerate_on_spell_start"
				"Target"				"POINT"
			}
			
			"ApplyModifier"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation"
	            "Target"				"CASTER"
	        }
		}

	    }

		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCooldown"				"25"
		"AbilityManaCost"				"100"
		"AbilityCastRange"				"250"  //Update cast_range if this is.
		"AoERadius"						"%wave_radius"
		"AbilityChannelTime"			"8.05"  //Update num_waves and delay_between_waves if this is.  An extra .05 channel time is added as a hack to get the last wave to deal damage.
		
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"					"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.vpcf"
			"soundfile"					"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_warlock.vsndevts"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"cast_range"						"40 80 120 160 200 240 280 320"  //Increases with Exort.  These values are currently hardcoded into AbilityCastRange because it cannot take in AbilitySpecial variables.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"num_waves"							"2 4 6 8 10 12 14 16"  //Increases with Exort.  Update AbilityChannelTime or delay_between_waves if this is.
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"wave_radius"						"50 100 150 200 250 300 350 400"  //Increases with Exort.
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"wave_radius_increase_per_wave"		"0"
			}
			"05"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"damage_per_wave"					"50"
			}
			"06"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"delay_between_waves"				".8"  //The first wave occurs this long after the channeling starts, and subsequent waves have this long of a delay between them, too.  Update AbilityChannelTime or num_waves if this is.
			}
			"07"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"channel_time"						"1.65 3.25 4.85 6.45 8.05 9.65 11.25 12.85"  //These values are currently hardcoded into AbilityChannelTime because it cannot take in AbilitySpecial variables.
			}
			"08"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"						"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.lua"
				"Function"				"invoker_retro_incinerate_on_spell_start"
				"Target"				"POINT"
			}
			
			"ApplyModifier"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation"
	            "Target"				"CASTER"
	        }
		}
		
		"OnChannelFinish"
	    {
	        "RemoveModifier"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation"
	            "Target"				"CASTER"
	        }
			
			"RemoveModifier"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation_override"
	            "Target"				"CASTER"
	        }
			
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.lua"
				"Function"				"invoker_retro_incinerate_on_channel_finish"
			}
	    }
		
		
		"Modifiers"
	    {
			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling"  //Applied to the dummy unit when Invoker begins channeling, and is removed when he stops.
	        {
				"Passive"			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"1"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				
	            "OnCreated"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.lua"
						"Function"				"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_on_created"
						"DelayBetweenWaves"		"%delay_between_waves"
						"DamagePerWave"			"%damage_per_wave"
					}
				}
	        }
			
	        "modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation"  //Repeatedly applies an animation to the caster to make them appear to be channeling.
	        {
				"Passive"			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"1"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				
	            "ThinkInterval"		".6"
	            "OnIntervalThink"
				{
	                "ApplyModifier"
	                {
	                    "ModifierName"		"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation_override"
	                    "Target"			"CASTER"
	                }
	            }
	        }
	
	        "modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation_override"
	        {
				"Duration"			"0.5"
	            "Passive"  			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"1"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				
	            "OverrideAnimation" "ACT_DOTA_CAST_ICE_WALL"
	        }
		}

		"AbilityChannelTime"			"1.65"  //Update num_waves and delay_between_waves if this is.  An extra .05 channel time is added as a hack to get the last wave to deal damage.

		{
			"particle"					"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.vpcf"
			"soundfile"					"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_warlock.vsndevts"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"cast_range"						"40 80 120 160 200 240 280 320"  //Increases with Exort.  These values are currently hardcoded into AbilityCastRange because it cannot take in AbilitySpecial variables.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"num_waves"							"2 4 6 8 10 12 14 16"  //Increases with Exort.  Update AbilityChannelTime or delay_between_waves if this is.
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"wave_radius"						"50 100 150 200 250 300 350 400"  //Increases with Exort.
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"wave_radius_increase_per_wave"		"0"
			}
			"05"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"damage_per_wave"					"50"
			}
			"06"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"delay_between_waves"				".8"  //The first wave occurs this long after the channeling starts, and subsequent waves have this long of a delay between them, too.  Update AbilityChannelTime or num_waves if this is.
			}
			"07"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"channel_time"						"1.65 3.25 4.85 6.45 8.05 9.65 11.25 12.85"  //These values are currently hardcoded into AbilityChannelTime because it cannot take in AbilitySpecial variables.
			}
			"08"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"						"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.lua"
				"Function"				"invoker_retro_incinerate_on_spell_start"
				"Target"				"POINT"
			}
			
			"ApplyModifier"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation"
	            "Target"				"CASTER"
	        }
		}

	    {
	        "RemoveModifier"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation"

			}
	    }

	    {

					}
				}
	        }

				"channel_time"						"1.65 3.25 4.85 6.45 8.05 9.65 11.25 12.85"  //These values are currently hardcoded into AbilityChannelTime because it cannot take in AbilitySpecial variables.
			}
			"08"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"						"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.lua"
				"Function"				"invoker_retro_incinerate_on_spell_start"
				"Target"				"POINT"
			}
			
			"ApplyModifier"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation"
	            "Target"				"CASTER"
	        }
		}
		
		"OnChannelFinish"
	    {
	        "RemoveModifier"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation"
	            "Target"				"CASTER"
	        }
			
			"RemoveModifier"
	        {
	            "ModifierName"			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation_override"
	            "Target"				"CASTER"
	        }
			
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_incinerate.lua"
				"Function"				"invoker_retro_incinerate_on_channel_finish"
			}
	    }
		
		
		"Modifiers"
	    {
			"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling"  //Applied to the dummy unit when Invoker begins channeling, and is removed when he stops.
	        {
				"Passive"			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"1"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				
	            "OnCreated"
				{
					"RunScript"

					}
				}
	        }
			
	        "modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation"  //Repeatedly applies an animation to the caster to make them appear to be channeling.
	        {
				"Passive"			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"1"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"

	            "OnIntervalThink"
				{
	                "ApplyModifier"
	                {
	                    "ModifierName"		"modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation_override"
	                    "Target"			"CASTER"
	                }
	            }
	        }
	
	        "modifier_invoker_retro_incinerate_channeling_animation_override"
	        {
				"Duration"			"0.5"
	            "Passive"  			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"1"
				"IsBuff"			"0"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				
	            "OverrideAnimation" "ACT_DOTA_CAST_ICE_WALL"
	        }
		}

	// Invoker's Inferno
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: March 7, 2015
	// Invoke: Exort Exort Wex
	// Creates random firey hells around Invoker. The damage varies by Exort levels and the number of Infernoes varies by Wex level.
	// This spell is split up into 8 versions for tooltip purposes.
	
	
	
	//Dummy for popup
	"invoker_retro_inferno"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NO_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NOT_LEARNABLE"

		"MaxLevel"						"1"
		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

		"AbilityManaCost"				"250"

		}

		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"num_infernos"						"1 2 3 4 5 6 7 8"  //Increases with Wex.  These values are hardcoded into the tooltip so the spell level can scale off of Exort.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"inferno_damage_per_second"			"30 37.5 45 52.5 60 67.5 75 82.5"  //Increases with Exort.
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"inferno_delay_between_spawns"		"1"  //The time between when the pre-explosion circles appear.  The first inferno's pre-explosion circle appears as soon as the ability is cast.
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"inferno_explosion_delay"			"2"  //The time between when the pre-explosion circle appears and when the inferno explodes.
			}
			"05"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"inferno_explosion_duration"		"2.67"  //Each inferno remains in effect and deals AoE damage for this long.
			}
			"06"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"inferno_spawn_radius"				"200"  //When infernos spawn, they will be centered at a random point within this many units from Invoker.
			}
			"07"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"inferno_radius"					"300"  //Infernos deal damage in this radius.
			}
			"08"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"inferno_damage_interval"			".5"
			}
			"09"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"			"1"
			}
		}

		{
			"RunScript"
			{

				"InfernoExplosionDelay"		"%inferno_explosion_delay"

				"InfernoRadius"				"%inferno_radius"
				"InfernoDelayBetweenSpawns"	"%inferno_delay_between_spawns"
			}
		}

		{

		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"num_infernos"						"1 2 3 4 5 6 7 8"  //Increases with Wex.  These values are hardcoded into the tooltip so the spell level can scale off of Exort.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"inferno_damage_per_second"			"30 37.5 45 52.5 60 67.5 75 82.5"  //Increases with Exort.
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"inferno_delay_between_spawns"		"1"  //The time between when the pre-explosion circles appear.  The first inferno's pre-explosion circle appears as soon as the ability is cast.
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"inferno_explosion_delay"			"2"  //The time between when the pre-explosion circle appears and when the inferno explodes.
			}
			"05"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"inferno_explosion_duration"		"2.67"  //Each inferno remains in effect and deals AoE damage for this long.
			}
			"06"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"inferno_spawn_radius"				"200"  //When infernos spawn, they will be centered at a random point within this many units from Invoker.
			}
			"07"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"inferno_radius"					"300"  //Infernos deal damage in this radius.
			}
			"08"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"inferno_damage_interval"			".5"
			}
			"09"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"			"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"				"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_inferno.lua"
				"Function"					"invoker_retro_inferno_on_spell_start"
				"InfernoSpawnRadius"		"%inferno_spawn_radius"
				"InfernoExplosionDelay"		"%inferno_explosion_delay"
				"InfernoExplosionDuration"	"%inferno_explosion_duration"
				"InfernoRadius"				"%inferno_radius"
				"InfernoDelayBetweenSpawns"	"%inferno_delay_between_spawns"
			}
		}
		
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_invoker_retro_inferno_damage_over_time"
			{
				"Passive"  			"0"
				"IsHidden" 			"1"

				"IsDebuff"			"0"

				"IsDebuff"			"1"

				"inferno_delay_between_spawns"		"1"  //The time between when the pre-explosion circles appear.  The first inferno's pre-explosion circle appears as soon as the ability is cast.
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"inferno_explosion_delay"			"2"  //The time between when the pre-explosion circle appears and when the inferno explodes.
			}
			"05"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"inferno_explosion_duration"		"2.67"  //Each inferno remains in effect and deals AoE damage for this long.
			}
			"06"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"inferno_spawn_radius"				"200"  //When infernos spawn, they will be centered at a random point within this many units from Invoker.
			}
			"07"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"inferno_radius"					"300"  //Infernos deal damage in this radius.
			}
			"08"
			{
				"var_type"							"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"inferno_damage_interval"			".5"
			}
			"09"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"			"1"

	// Invoker's Invisibility Aura
	// Author: Rook and wFX
	// Date: February 24, 2015
	// Invoke: Quas Exort Wex
	// Units within 190 range of Kael become Invisible. Range based on Quas level
	"invoker_retro_invisibility_aura"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"

		{

		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"radius"				"150 170 190 210 230 250 270 290"  //Increases with Quas.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"fade_time"				".7"
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"

		}

		{
			"modifier_invoker_retro_invisibility_aura"

					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_invisibility_aura.lua"
						"Function"		"modifier_invoker_retro_invisibility_aura_on_interval_think"
						"FadeTime"		"%fade_time"
					}
				}
				
				"OnCreated"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_invisibility_aura.lua"
						"Function"		"modifier_invoker_retro_invisibility_aura_on_created"
					}
				}
				
				"OnDestroy"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_invisibility_aura.lua"
						"Function"		"modifier_invoker_retro_invisibility_aura_on_destroy"
					}
				}
			}
			
			//A modifier this is applied to units while they are within the radius of a friendly Invoker's Invisibility Aura.
			"modifier_invoker_retro_invisibility_aura_in_radius"
			{
				"Duration"			".5"
				"Passive"  			"0"
				"IsHidden"			"1"
				
				"OnAbilityExecuted"  //Remove the invisibility modifier from this unit (if applicable).
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_invisibility_aura.lua"
						"Function"		"modifier_invoker_retro_invisibility_aura_in_radius_on_ability_executed"
					}
				}
				
				//Note: For parity, the invisibility should be removed when the autoattack projectile appears, 
				//but there is currently no event that can be used for this.
				"OnAttackStart" 
				{				
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_invisibility_aura.lua"
						"Function"		"modifier_invoker_retro_invisibility_aura_in_radius_on_attack_start"
					}
				}
			}
			
			"modifier_invoker_retro_invisibility_aura_effect"
			{
				"Passive"			"0"
				"IsHidden"			"0"
				"IsBuff"			"1"
				"IsDebuff"			"0"
				"IsPurgable"		"0"
				"Duration"			".5"
				"Attributes"		"MODIFIER_ATTRIBUTE_IGNORE_INVULNERABLE"
				"TextureName"		"invoker_retro_invisibility_aura"
	
				"States"
				{
					"MODIFIER_STATE_INVISIBLE"					"MODIFIER_STATE_VALUE_ENABLED"
				}
				
				"ThinkInterval" 		".03"
				//Repeatedly apply the stock modifier_invisible for the sole purpose of making the unit have a transparent texture.
				//This can be gotten rid of when we discover how to apply a translucent texture manually.
				"OnIntervalThink"
				{
					"RunScript"
					{
						"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_invisibility_aura.lua"
						"Function"		"modifier_invoker_retro_invisibility_aura_effect_on_interval_think"
					}
				}
			}
		}

	// Invoker's Levitation
	// Author: Rook, with help from Noya's code
	// Date: February 19, 2015
	// Invoke: Quas Wex Exort
	// Allows you to rise into the air, invulnerable. Duration is based on Wex, Quas and Exort.
	// Balance ideas: While levitating, replace the skill with a sub-ability that allows you to cancel the levitation early.

	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

	// Invoker's Lightning Shield

	// Invoker's Portal
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: February 18, 2015
	// Invoke: Quas Quas Wex
	// Casts a powerful displacement magic at another unit. Deals damage to it. That unit is instantly moved to your position.  Cast range is based on Quas, damage based on Wex.
	// Because Quas affects the AbilityCastRange, we use a separate ability for each possible Quas level.
	
	
	
	//Dummy for popup

	// Invoker's Power Word
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: February 23, 2015
	// Invoke: Quas Exort Quas
	// Applies a magic that weakes or strengthens a unit's resistance to physical attacks. Increases a friendly unit's armor or decreaes an enemy's armor by 3. Lasts 25 seconds
	// Balance ideas: Make use of Exort's level somehow.
	"invoker_retro_power_word"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_UNIT_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NOT_LEARNABLE"
		"AbilityUnitTargetTeam"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_BOTH"
		"AbilityUnitTargetType"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_CREEP"
		"AbilityTextureName" 			"invoker_retro_power_word"
		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_NO"
		"AbilityCastAnimation" 			"ACT_DOTA_CAST_ALACRITY"
		"FightRecapLevel"				"1"
		"MaxLevel"						"1"
		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCooldown"				"30"
		"AbilityManaCost"				"200"
		"AbilityCastRange"				"650"
		
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"					"particles/units/heroes/hero_dazzle/dazzle_armor_friend_shield.vpcf"
			"particle"					"particles/units/heroes/hero_dazzle/dazzle_armor_enemy_shield.vpcf"
			"particle"					"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_power_word_ally.vpcf"
			"particle"                  "particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_power_word_enemy.vpcf"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"armor_bonus_ally"		"1 2 3 4 5 6 7 8"
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"armor_reduction_enemy"	"-1 -2 -3 -4 -5 -6 -7 -8"
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"duration"				"25"
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"			"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"			"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_power_word.lua"
				"Function"				"invoker_retro_power_word_on_spell_start"
			}
		}
		
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_invoker_retro_power_word_armor_debuff_icon"  //When cast on enemies.  This icon will appear on their modifier bar.
			{
				"Duration"				"%duration"
				"Passive"				"0"
				"IsHidden"				"0"
				"IsBuff"				"0"
				"IsDebuff"				"1"
				"IsPurgable"			"1"
				"EffectName"			"particles/units/heroes/hero_dazzle/dazzle_armor_enemy_shield.vpcf"
				"EffectAttachType"		"follow_overhead"
				"TextureName"			"invoker_retro_power_word"
			}
			"modifier_invoker_retro_power_word_armor_debuff"  //When cast on enemies.  
			{
				"Duration"				"%duration"
				"Passive"				"0"
				"IsHidden"				"1"
				"IsBuff"				"0"
				"IsDebuff"				"1"
				"IsPurgable"			"1"
				"Attributes" 			"MODIFIER_ATTRIBUTE_MULTIPLE"
				
				"Properties"
				{
					"MODIFIER_PROPERTY_PHYSICAL_ARMOR_BONUS"		"-1"
				}
			}
			"modifier_invoker_retro_power_word_armor_buff_icon"  //When cast on allies.  This icon will appear on their modifier bar.
			{
				"Duration"				"%duration"
				"Passive"				"0"
				"IsHidden"				"0"
				"IsBuff"				"1"
				"IsDebuff"				"0"
				"IsPurgable"			"1"

	// Invoker's Quas
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: February 15, 2015
	// Builds Kael's skills in the arcana magics. These spells, when invoked deal with the power of the mind, wind and water. As a regeant, increases damage by 2% per level, per regeant cast. Increases Intelligence by 1 each time this skill is learned.
	"invoker_retro_quas"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NO_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_IMMEDIATE | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_IGNORE_BACKSWING"
		"AbilityTextureName" 			"invoker_retro_quas"
		"MaxLevel"						"8"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

		"AbilityManaCost"				"0"

			"soundfile"			"soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_invoker.vsndevts"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"								"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"bonus_damage_percent_per_instance"		"2 4 6 8 10 12 14 16"
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"								"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"bonus_intelligence"					"1 2 3 4 5 6 7 8"
			}
			"03"
			{

			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{

			}
		}

	// Invoker's Shroud of Flames
	// Author: Noya
	// Date: February 15, 2015
	// Invoke: Quas Exort Exort
	// Creates a barrier that reduces spell damage against a friendly unit by 12%. Units that attack that unit get flamed, with damage based on Exort. Lasts 40 seconds.
	
	
	
	//Dummy for popup
	"invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames"
	{
	    // General
	    //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	    "BaseClass"                     "ability_datadriven"
	    "AbilityBehavior"               "DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_UNIT_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NOT_LEARNABLE"
	    "AbilityUnitTargetTeam"         "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_FRIENDLY"
	    "AbilityUnitTargetType"         "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_BASIC"
	    "AbilityTextureName"            "invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames"
	    "AbilityUnitDamageType"         "DAMAGE_TYPE_MAGICAL"
	    "AbilityCastAnimation"          "ACT_DOTA_CAST_ICE_WALL"
	    "MaxLevel"                      "1"
		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"
	    
	    // Stats
	    //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	    "AbilityCooldown"               "30"
	    "AbilityManaCost"               "250"
	    "AbilityCastRange"              "500"
	    "AbilityDuration"               "40" //Tooltip states "Lasts 40 seconds"
	    
	    "precache"
	    {
	        "particle"  "particles/units/heroes/hero_dragon_knight/dragon_knight_breathe_fire.vpcf"
	        "particle"  "particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames.vpcf"
	        "soundfile" "soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_ember_spirit.vsndevts"
	        "soundfile" "soundevents/game_sounds_heroes/game_sounds_dragon_knight.vsndevts"
	    }
	    
	    // Special
	    //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	    "AbilitySpecial"
	    {
	        "01"
	        {
	            "var_type"              "FIELD_FLOAT"
	            "magic_resistance"      "4 8 12 16 20 24 28 32" // Scales with Quas
	        }
	        "02"
	        {
	            "var_type"              "FIELD_INTEGER"
	            "damage_exort"          "8 16 24 32 40 48 56 64" // Scales with Exort. Hardcoded tooltip
	        }
	        "03"
	        {
	            "var_type"              "FIELD_FLOAT"
	            "pip_current"           "1"
	        }
	    }
	
	    "OnSpellStart"
	    {
	        // Create a dummy, which will learn this ability and apply the modifier on the target
	        "RunScript"
	        {
	            "ScriptFile"    "heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames.lua"
	            "Function"      "invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames_dummy"
	        }
	        "FireSound"
	        {
	            "EffectName"    "Hero_EmberSpirit.FlameGuard.Cast"
	            "Target"        "TARGET"
	        }
	    }
	
	    "OnProjectileHitUnit"
	    {
	        "DeleteOnHit" "0"
	        "RunScript"
	        {
	            "ScriptFile"    "heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames.lua"
	            "Function"      "invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames"
	        }
	    }
	
	    "Modifiers"
	    {
	        "modifier_shroud_of_flames"
	        {
	            "TextureName"   "invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames"
	            "Duration"      "%AbilityDuration"
	            "Properties"
	            {
	                    "MODIFIER_PROPERTY_MAGICAL_RESISTANCE_BONUS" "%magic_resistance"
	            }
	
	            "OnCreated"
	            {
	                "AttachEffect"
	                {
	                    "Target"              "TARGET"
	                    "EffectName"          "particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames.vpcf"
	                    "EffectAttachType"    "start_at_customorigin"
	                    "ControlPointEntities"
	                    {
	                        "TARGET"     "attach_origin"
	                        "TARGET"     "attach_origin"
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	
	            "OnAttacked"
	            {
	                "LinearProjectile"
	                {
	                    "Target"        "ATTACKER"
	                    "Source"        "TARGET"
	                    "EffectName"    "particles/units/heroes/hero_dragon_knight/dragon_knight_breathe_fire.vpcf"
	                    "MoveSpeed"     "900"
	                    "StartRadius"   "100"
	                    "StartPosition" "attach_origin"
	                    "EndRadius"     "500"
	                    "FixedDistance" "600"
	                    "TargetTeams"   "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_ENEMY"
	                    "TargetTypes"   "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_BASIC | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_MECHANICAL"
	                    "TargetFlags"   "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_FLAG_NONE"
	                    "HasFrontalCone" "1"
	                    "ProvidesVision" "0"
	                }
	            }
	        }
	    }
	}

	        }
	    }

	            }

	                {

		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"magic_resistance"		"4 8 12 16 20 24 28 32"	// Scales with Quas
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"damage_exort"			"8 16 24 32 40 48 56 64" // Scales with Exort. Hardcoded tooltip
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"			"1"
			}
		}
	
		"OnSpellStart"
	    {
	    	// Create a dummy, which will learn this ability and apply the modifier on the target
	    	"RunScript"
	    	{
	    		"ScriptFile"	"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames.lua"
	    		"Function"		"invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames_dummy"
	    	}
	        "FireSound"
	        {
	            "EffectName"    "Hero_EmberSpirit.FlameGuard.Cast"
	            "Target"        "TARGET"
	        }
	    }
	
	    "OnProjectileHitUnit"
	    {
	        "DeleteOnHit" "0"
	        "RunScript"
	        {
	            "ScriptFile"    "heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames.lua"
	            "Function"      "invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames"
	        }
	    }
	
	    "Modifiers"
	    {
	        "modifier_shroud_of_flames"
	        {
	        	"TextureName"	"invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames"
	        	"Duration"		"%AbilityDuration"
	            "Properties"
	            {
	                    "MODIFIER_PROPERTY_MAGICAL_RESISTANCE_BONUS" "%magic_resistance"
	            }
	
	            "OnCreated"
	            {
			        "AttachEffect"
	                {
	                    "Target"              "TARGET"
	                    "EffectName"          "particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_shroud_of_flames.vpcf"
	                    "EffectAttachType"    "start_at_customorigin"
	                    "ControlPointEntities"
	                    {
	                        "TARGET"     "attach_origin"
	                        "TARGET"     "attach_origin"
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	
	            "OnAttacked"
	            {
	            	"LinearProjectile"
			        {
		                "Target"        "ATTACKER"
		                "Source"		"TARGET"
		                "EffectName"    "particles/units/heroes/hero_dragon_knight/dragon_knight_breathe_fire.vpcf"
		                "MoveSpeed"     "900"
		                "StartRadius"   "100"
		                "StartPosition" "attach_origin"
		                "EndRadius"     "500"
		                "FixedDistance" "600"
		                "TargetTeams"   "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_ENEMY"
		                "TargetTypes"   "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_BASIC | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_MECHANICAL"
		                "TargetFlags"   "DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_FLAG_NONE"
		                "HasFrontalCone" "1"
		                "ProvidesVision" "0"
			        }
	            }
	        }
	    }
	}
	// Invoker's Soul Blast
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: February 25, 2015
	// Invoke: Wex Quas Exort
	// Deals up to 600 damage to a target enemy unit, based on Exort. Heals the Invoker for up to 500 hit points, based on Quas. Cast range is based on Wex.
	// Because Wex affects the AbilityCastRange, we use a separate ability for each possible Wex level.
	
	
	
	//Dummy for popup
	"invoker_retro_soul_blast"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_UNIT_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NOT_LEARNABLE"
		"AbilityUnitTargetTeam"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_TEAM_ENEMY"
		"AbilityUnitTargetType"			"DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_HERO | DOTA_UNIT_TARGET_CREEP"
		"AbilityTextureName" 			"invoker_retro_soul_blast"
		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_NO"
		"AbilityUnitDamageType"			"DAMAGE_TYPE_MAGICAL"
		"AbilityCastAnimation" 			"ACT_DOTA_CAST_COLD_SNAP"
		"FightRecapLevel"				"1"
		"MaxLevel"						"1"

		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"damage"				"75 150 225 300 375 450 525 600"  //Increases with Exort.  These values are hardcoded into the tooltip.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"heal"					"62.5 125 187.5 250 312.5 375 437.5 500"  //Increases with Quas.  These values are hardcoded into the tooltip.
			}
			"03"

				"cast_range"			"400 448 496 544 592 640 688 736"  //Increases with Wex.  This value is hardcoded into each ability's AbilityCastRange.

			}

	// Invoker's Soul Reaver

	// Invoke: Exort Wex Quas

	// Invoker's Tornado Blast
	// Author: Rook
	// Date: February 19, 2015
	// Invoke: Quas Wex Wex
	// Summons a tornado to wreak havoc and damage enemy units over a long distance. Deals 225 damage over 750 range.
	// Balance ideas: Travel distance should scale with Wex instead of Quas.  The tornado could also pick up enemies
	//     like it does in Dota's modern Invoker incarnation.
	// Because Quas affects the AbilityCastRange, we use a separate ability for each possible Quas level.
	
	
	
	//Dummy for Popup
	"invoker_retro_tornado_blast"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_POINT | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NOT_LEARNABLE"
		"AbilityTextureName" 			"invoker_retro_tornado_blast"
		"SpellImmunityType"				"SPELL_IMMUNITY_ENEMIES_NO"
		"AbilityUnitDamageType"			"DAMAGE_TYPE_MAGICAL"
		"AbilityCastAnimation" 			"ACT_DOTA_CAST_TORNADO"
		"FightRecapLevel"				"1"
		"MaxLevel"						"1"
		"AbilityProcsMagicStick" 		"1"
		
		// Stats
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCooldown"				"25"
		"AbilityManaCost"				"250"
		"AbilityCastRange"				"250"
		
		"precache"
		{
			"particle"			"particles/units/heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_tornado.vpcf"
		}
		
		// Special
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilitySpecial"
		{
			"01"
			{
				"var_type"										"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"damage"										"125 175 225 275 325 375 425 475"  //Increases with Quas.
			}
			"02"
			{
				"var_type"										"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"travel_distance"								"250 500 750 1000 1250 1500 1750 2000"  //Increases with Quas.  This value is hardcoded into each ability's AbilityCastRange.
			}
			"03"
			{
				"var_type"										"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"projectile_speed"								"1000"
			}
			"04"
			{
				"var_type"										"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"projectile_radius"								"200"
			}
			"05"
			{
				"var_type"										"FIELD_INTEGER"
				"projectile_flying_vision"						"600"
			}
			"06"
			{
				"var_type"										"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"projectile_flying_vision_max_range_duration"	"1.75"
			}
			"07"
			{
				"var_type"				"FIELD_FLOAT"
				"pip_current"			"1"
			}
		}
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"								"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_tornado_blast.lua"
				"Function"									"invoker_retro_tornado_blast_on_spell_start"
				"Target"									"POINT"
				"ProjectileSpeed"							"%projectile_speed"
				"ProjectileRadius"							"%projectile_radius"
				"ProjectileFlyingVision"					"%projectile_flying_vision"
				"ProjectileFlyingVisionMaxRangeDuration"	"%projectile_flying_vision_max_range_duration"
			}
		}
		
		"OnProjectileHitUnit"
		{
			"DeleteOnHit" "0"
			
			"RunScript"
			{
				"ScriptFile"		"heroes/hero_invoker/invoker_retro_tornado_blast.lua"
				"Function"			"invoker_retro_tornado_blast_on_projectile_hit_unit"
			}
		}
	}
